# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repositories (version-pinned mirrors):**

- `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-kubernetes` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-kubernetes$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-client-go` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-client-go$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-api` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-api$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd$` filter

Scope ALL keyword_search/nls_search queries to these repos.
Use the repo name as the `repo` parameter for read_file/go_to_definition/find_references.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

---

**Sourcegraph Repositories:** `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-kubernetes`, `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-client-go`, `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-api`, `github.com/sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd`

# Kubernetes Admission Webhook Processing Chain

## Your Task

Trace the admission webhook processing chain in Kubernetes. Find Go source files across kubernetes/kubernetes and kubernetes/api that implement: the generic Webhook dispatcher (in pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/), the mutating webhook dispatcher with reinvocation logic, the validating webhook dispatcher with parallel dispatch, the WebhookAccessor abstraction layer, and the MutatingWebhookConfiguration/ValidatingWebhookConfiguration API type definitions.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo tracing domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` (etcd-io/etcd)

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [

  ],

}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Summary of Findings

### Key Components Identified:

1. **WebhookAccessor Abstraction Layer** - A unified interface for both mutating and validating webhooks that abstracts away type differences
   - `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go`

2. **Generic Webhook Dispatcher Foundation** - Base infrastructure for admission webhook processing
   - `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go`
   - `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/interfaces.go`

3. **Mutating Webhook Dispatcher** - Sequential processing with sophisticated reinvocation logic
   - `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go`
   - `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/reinvocationcontext.go`
   - Tracks previously invoked webhooks and reinvokes them when objects change

4. **Validating Webhook Dispatcher** - Parallel processing for performance
   - `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go`
   - Uses goroutines with WaitGroup for concurrent webhook invocation

5. **Configuration Managers** - Dynamic loading of webhook configurations
   - `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go`
   - `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go`

6. **API Type Definitions** - Resource definitions in kubernetes-api
   - `admissionregistration/v1/types.go` - MutatingWebhookConfiguration, ValidatingWebhookConfiguration
   - `admissionregistration/v1beta1/types.go` - Depreca

Chain\\n\\n### Overview\\nThe admission webhook processing chain in Kubernetes is implemented across multiple interconnected components that handle both mutating and validating webhooks. The chain follows a generic dispatcher pattern with specialized implementations for each webhook type.\\n\\n### Core Abstraction Layer: WebhookAccessor\\n\\nThe **WebhookAccessor** interface (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go`) provides a unified abstraction for both mutating and validating webhook types. It defines methods for:\\n- Accessing webhook metadata (name, UID, configuration name)\\n- Retrieving webhook configuration (rules, failure policy, match policy, selectors)\\n- Obtaining REST clients and compiled matchers for CEL expressions\\n- Determining webhook type (mutating vs validating)\\n\\nThe interface has two concrete implementations:\\n- **mutatingWebhookAccessor** wraps `v1.MutatingWebhook`\\n- **validatingWebhookAccessor** wraps `v1.ValidatingWebhook`\\n\\nFactory functions `NewMutatingWebhookAccessor()` and `NewValidatingWebhookAccessor()` create these accessors with a unique ID and configuration name.\\n\\n### API Type Definitions\\n\\nThe API types are defined in the `kubernetes-api` repository:\\n\\n**v1 API** (`admissionregistration/v1/types.go`):\\n- **MutatingWebhookConfiguration**: Describes admission webhooks that can modify resources\\n- **MutatingWebhook**: Individual webhook entry with client config, rules, and policies\\n- **ValidatingWebhookConfiguration**: Describes admission webhooks that validate resources without modification\\n- **ValidatingWebhook**: Individual validating webhook entry with similar structure to MutatingWebhook\\n\\n**v1beta1 API** (`admissionregistration/v1beta1/types.go`):\\n- Deprecated versions of the above types, maintained for backward compatibility\\n\\nKey webhook fields include:\\n- `ClientConfig`: Connection details (URL or Kubernetes service reference)\\n- `Rules`: Which operations and resources trigger the webhook\\n- `FailurePolicy`: Whether to fail open or closed on webhook errors\\n- `MatchPolicy`: Exact or equivalent matching for rules\\n- `NamespaceSelector` and `ObjectSelector`: Label-based filtering\\n- `AdmissionReviewVersions`: Supported API review versions\\n- `MatchConditions`: CEL-based filtering expressions\\n\\n### Configuration Managers\\n\\nConfiguration managers implement the **Source** interface and manage loading webhook configurations from the API server:\\n\\n**MutatingWebhookConfigurationManager** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go`):\\n- Watches MutatingWebhookConfiguration objects via informer\\n- Converts configurations into WebhookAccessor instances\\n- Caches compiled matchers (CEL expressions) to avoid recompilation\\n- Implements lazy evaluation with cache invalidation on updates\\n\\n**ValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go`):\\n- Similar functionality for ValidatingWebhookConfiguration objects\\n- Manages ValidatingWebhookConfiguration informer\\n- Maintains deterministic ordering of webhooks by sorting configurations\\n\\nBoth managers use `synctrack.Lazy` for deferred evaluation and implement efficient caching strategies.\\n\\n### Generic Webhook Dispatcher Foundation\\n\\nThe **Webhook** class (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go`) provides the base admission plugin infrastructure:\\n\\n- Initializes with a source factory (configuration manager) and dispatcher factory\\n- Manages webhook source (provides list of active webhooks)\\n- Coordinates with dispatchers for actual webhook invocation\\n- Handles namespace and object matching via predicates\\n- Compiles and executes CEL match conditions\\n\\nKey interfaces defined in `generic/interfaces.go`:\\n\\n**Dispatcher** interface: Dispatches requests to a list of webhooks\\n- `Dispatch(ctx, attributes, objectInterfaces, hooks) error`: Process webhooks for a request\\n\\n**Source** interface: Provides active webhooks\\n- `Webhooks() []WebhookAccessor`: List of active webhooks\\n- `HasSynced() bool`: Whether configuration is synced\\n\\n**WebhookInvocation**: Describes how to call a specific webhook\\n- `Webhook`: The WebhookAccessor instance\\n- `Resource`: GroupVersionResource the webhook was registered for\\n- `Kind`: GroupVersionKind to send to the webhook\\n- `Subresource`: Subresource if applicable\\n\\n**VersionedAttributeAccessor**: Provides versioned admission attributes\\n- `VersionedAttribute(gvk) *VersionedAttributes`: Get attributes in requested version\\n\\n### Mutating Webhook Dispatcher with Reinvocation Logic\\n\\nThe **mutatingDispatcher** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go`) implements mutation with reinvocation support:\\n\\n**Sequential Processing**:\\n- Mutating webhooks are called in order, one at a time\\n- Each webhook can modify the object being admitted\\n- Modifications are passed to subsequent webhooks\\n\\n**Reinvocation Mechanism** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/reinvocationcontext.go`):\\n- Tracks previously invoked webhooks via `webhookReinvokeContext`\\n- When in-tree admission plugins mutate the object, webhooks are reinvoked\\n- Maintains `lastWebhookOutput` to detect if object changed since last webhook\\n- Maintains `previouslyInvokedReinvocableWebhooks` set for reinvocation\\n- Prevents infinite loops by only reinvoking webhooks that previously ran\\n\\n**Key reinvocation logic**:\\n- Detects object changes using deep equality comparison\\n- Reinvokes all previously invoked webhooks if object changed\\n- Skips webhooks that didn't match in the first round\\n- Stores reinvocation state in `admission.ReinvocationContext`\\n\\n**Plugin Registration** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go`):\\n- Registered as \\\"MutatingAdmissionWebhook\\\"\\n- Implements `admission.MutationInterface`\\n- Creates generic.Webhook with MutatingWebhookConfigurationManager and mutatingDispatcher\\n\\n### Validating Webhook Dispatcher with Parallel Dispatch\\n\\nThe **validatingDispatcher** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go`) implements validation with parallel execution:\\n\\n**Parallel Processing**:\\n- Validating webhooks are called concurrently using goroutines\\n- Uses `sync.WaitGroup` to coordinate goroutine completion\\n- Collects errors via buffered error channel (2x webhook count)\\n- First matching rejection error terminates dispatch\\n\\n**Efficiency Optimizations**:\\n- Pre-converts admission attributes to required versions before parallel dispatch\\n- Caches versioned attributes to avoid redundant conversions\\n- Checks context timeout before spawning goroutines\\n- Uses panic recovery to prevent goroutine failures from crashing apiserver\\n\\n**Error Handling**:\\n- Handles both webhook call failures and panics\\n- Respects failure policy (Ignore vs Fail)\\n- Logs failures with appropriate severity levels\\n- Properly joins goroutines before returning\\n\\n**Plugin Registration** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go`):\\n- Registered as \\\"ValidatingAdmissionWebhook\\\"\\n- Implements `admission.ValidationInterface`\\n- Creates generic.Webhook with ValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager and validatingDispatcher\\n\\n### Processing Chain Flow\\n\\n1. **Initialization**:\\n   - Plugin registers and creates generic.Webhook\\n   - Configuration manager watches API server for webhook configurations\\n   - Source factory creates configuration manager instance\\n   - Dispatcher factory creates appropriate dispatcher (mutating or validating)\\n\\n2. **Configuration Loading**:\\n   - Informer watches MutatingWebhookConfiguration or ValidatingWebhookConfiguration\\n   - Changes trigger cache invalidation and recompilation of CEL expressions\\n   - WebhookAccessor instances created with compiled matchers\\n\\n3. **Request Processing**:\\n   - Admission request arrives at generic.Webhook\\n   - Source provides current list of active webhooks\\n   - Dispatcher iterates through webhooks:\\n     - Matches rules against request\\n     - Evaluates namespace/object selectors\\n     - Executes CEL match conditions\\n     - Invokes matching webhooks\\n   - For mutating: Sequential processing with reinvocation support\\n   - For validating: Parallel processing with timeout handling\\n\\n4. **Response Handling**:\\n   - Mutations collected and applied to request\\n   - Validation errors rejected based on failure policy\\n   - Errors aggregated and returned to caller\\n\\n### Key Design Patterns\\n\\n**Abstraction**: WebhookAccessor unifies mutating and validating webhook handling\\n**Factory Pattern**: Source and Dispatcher factories enable dependency injection and testing\\n**Informer Pattern**: Configuration managers use SharedInformerFactory for efficient API watching\\n**Lazy Evaluation**: Configuration compilation deferred until first use and cached\\n**Parallel Execution**: Validating webhooks exploit concurrency for performance\\n**Reinvocation**: Mutating webhooks support re-evaluation when object changes\\n**CEL Matching**: Match conditions compiled once and reused for each request\\n\"\n}\n",

Chain\\n\\n### Overview\\nThe admission webhook processing chain in Kubernetes is implemented across multiple interconnected components that handle both mutating and validating webhooks. The chain follows a generic dispatcher pattern with specialized implementations for each webhook type.\\n\\n### Core Abstraction Layer: WebhookAccessor\\n\\nThe **WebhookAccessor** interface (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go`) provides a unified abstraction for both mutating and validating webhook types. It defines methods for:\\n- Accessing webhook metadata (name, UID, configuration name)\\n- Retrieving webhook configuration (rules, failure policy, match policy, selectors)\\n- Obtaining REST clients and compiled matchers for CEL expressions\\n- Determining webhook type (mutating vs validating)\\n\\nThe interface has two concrete implementations:\\n- **mutatingWebhookAccessor** wraps `v1.MutatingWebhook`\\n- **validatingWebhookAccessor** wraps `v1.ValidatingWebhook`\\n\\nFactory functions `NewMutatingWebhookAccessor()` and `NewValidatingWebhookAccessor()` create these accessors with a unique ID and configuration name.\\n\\n### API Type Definitions\\n\\nThe API types are defined in the `kubernetes-api` repository:\\n\\n**v1 API** (`admissionregistration/v1/types.go`):\\n- **MutatingWebhookConfiguration**: Describes admission webhooks that can modify resources\\n- **MutatingWebhook**: Individual webhook entry with client config, rules, and policies\\n- **ValidatingWebhookConfiguration**: Describes admission webhooks that validate resources without modification\\n- **ValidatingWebhook**: Individual validating webhook entry with similar structure to MutatingWebhook\\n\\n**v1beta1 API** (`admissionregistration/v1beta1/types.go`):\\n- Deprecated versions of the above types, maintained for backward compatibility\\n\\nKey webhook fields include:\\n- `ClientConfig`: Connection details (URL or Kubernetes service reference)\\n- `Rules`: Which operations and resources trigger the webhook\\n- `FailurePolicy`: Whether to fail open or closed on webhook errors\\n- `MatchPolicy`: Exact or equivalent matching for rules\\n- `NamespaceSelector` and `ObjectSelector`: Label-based filtering\\n- `AdmissionReviewVersions`: Supported API review versions\\n- `MatchConditions`: CEL-based filtering expressions\\n\\n### Configuration Managers\\n\\nConfiguration managers implement the **Source** interface and manage loading webhook configurations from the API server:\\n\\n**MutatingWebhookConfigurationManager** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go`):\\n- Watches MutatingWebhookConfiguration objects via informer\\n- Converts configurations into WebhookAccessor instances\\n- Caches compiled matchers (CEL expressions) to avoid recompilation\\n- Implements lazy evaluation with cache invalidation on updates\\n\\n**ValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go`):\\n- Similar functionality for ValidatingWebhookConfiguration objects\\n- Manages ValidatingWebhookConfiguration informer\\n- Maintains deterministic ordering of webhooks by sorting configurations\\n\\nBoth managers use `synctrack.Lazy` for deferred evaluation and implement efficient caching strategies.\\n\\n### Generic Webhook Dispatcher Foundation\\n\\nThe **Webhook** class (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go`) provides the base admission plugin infrastructure:\\n\\n- Initializes with a source factory (configuration manager) and dispatcher factory\\n- Manages webhook source (provides list of active webhooks)\\n- Coordinates with dispatchers for actual webhook invocation\\n- Handles namespace and object matching via predicates\\n- Compiles and executes CEL match conditions\\n\\nKey interfaces defined in `generic/interfaces.go`:\\n\\n**Dispatcher** interface: Dispatches requests to a list of webhooks\\n- `Dispatch(ctx, attributes, objectInterfaces, hooks) error`: Process webhooks for a request\\n\\n**Source** interface: Provides active webhooks\\n- `Webhooks() []WebhookAccessor`: List of active webhooks\\n- `HasSynced() bool`: Whether configuration is synced\\n\\n**WebhookInvocation**: Describes how to call a specific webhook\\n- `Webhook`: The WebhookAccessor instance\\n- `Resource`: GroupVersionResource the webhook was registered for\\n- `Kind`: GroupVersionKind to send to the webhook\\n- `Subresource`: Subresource if applicable\\n\\n**VersionedAttributeAccessor**: Provides versioned admission attributes\\n- `VersionedAttribute(gvk) *VersionedAttributes`: Get attributes in requested version\\n\\n### Mutating Webhook Dispatcher with Reinvocation Logic\\n\\nThe **mutatingDispatcher** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go`) implements mutation with reinvocation support:\\n\\n**Sequential Processing**:\\n- Mutating webhooks are called in order, one at a time\\n- Each webhook can modify the object being admitted\\n- Modifications are passed to subsequent webhooks\\n\\n**Reinvocation Mechanism** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/reinvocationcontext.go`):\\n- Tracks previously invoked webhooks via `webhookReinvokeContext`\\n- When in-tree admission plugins mutate the object, webhooks are reinvoked\\n- Maintains `lastWebhookOutput` to detect if object changed since last webhook\\n- Maintains `previouslyInvokedReinvocableWebhooks` set for reinvocation\\n- Prevents infinite loops by only reinvoking webhooks that previously ran\\n\\n**Key reinvocation logic**:\\n- Detects object changes using deep equality comparison\\n- Reinvokes all previously invoked webhooks if object changed\\n- Skips webhooks that didn't match in the first round\\n- Stores reinvocation state in `admission.ReinvocationContext`\\n\\n**Plugin Registration** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go`):\\n- Registered as \\\"MutatingAdmissionWebhook\\\"\\n- Implements `admission.MutationInterface`\\n- Creates generic.Webhook with MutatingWebhookConfigurationManager and mutatingDispatcher\\n\\n### Validating Webhook Dispatcher with Parallel Dispatch\\n\\nThe **validatingDispatcher** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go`) implements validation with parallel execution:\\n\\n**Parallel Processing**:\\n- Validating webhooks are called concurrently using goroutines\\n- Uses `sync.WaitGroup` to coordinate goroutine completion\\n- Collects errors via buffered error channel (2x webhook count)\\n- First matching rejection error terminates dispatch\\n\\n**Efficiency Optimizations**:\\n- Pre-converts admission attributes to required versions before parallel dispatch\\n- Caches versioned attributes to avoid redundant conversions\\n- Checks context timeout before spawning goroutines\\n- Uses panic recovery to prevent goroutine failures from crashing apiserver\\n\\n**Error Handling**:\\n- Handles both webhook call failures and panics\\n- Respects failure policy (Ignore vs Fail)\\n- Logs failures with appropriate severity levels\\n- Properly joins goroutines before returning\\n\\n**Plugin Registration** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go`):\\n- Registered as \\\"ValidatingAdmissionWebhook\\\"\\n- Implements `admission.ValidationInterface`\\n- Creates generic.Webhook with ValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager and validatingDispatcher\\n\\n### Processing Chain Flow\\n\\n1. **Initialization**:\\n   - Plugin registers and creates generic.Webhook\\n   - Configuration manager watches API server for webhook configurations\\n   - Source factory creates configuration manager instance\\n   - Dispatcher factory creates appropriate dispatcher (mutating or validating)\\n\\n2. **Configuration Loading**:\\n   - Informer watches MutatingWebhookConfiguration or ValidatingWebhookConfiguration\\n   - Changes trigger cache invalidation and recompilation of CEL expressions\\n   - WebhookAccessor instances created with compiled matchers\\n\\n3. **Request Processing**:\\n   - Admission request arrives at generic.Webhook\\n   - Source provides current list of active webhooks\\n   - Dispatcher iterates through webhooks:\\n     - Matches rules against request\\n     - Evaluates namespace/object selectors\\n     - Executes CEL match conditions\\n     - Invokes matching webhooks\\n   - For mutating: Sequential processing with reinvocation support\\n   - For validating: Parallel processing with timeout handling\\n\\n4. **Response Handling**:\\n   - Mutations collected and applied to request\\n   - Validation errors rejected based on failure policy\\n   - Errors aggregated and returned to caller\\n\\n### Key Design Patterns\\n\\n**Abstraction**: WebhookAccessor unifies mutating and validating webhook handling\\n**Factory Pattern**: Source and Dispatcher factories enable dependency injection and testing\\n**Informer Pattern**: Configuration managers use SharedInformerFactory for efficient API watching\\n**Lazy Evaluation**: Configuration compilation deferred until first use and cached\\n**Parallel Execution**: Validating webhooks exploit concurrency for performance\\n**Reinvocation**: Mutating webhooks support re-evaluation when object changes\\n**CEL Matching**: Match conditions compiled once and reused for each request\\n\"\n}\n",
